   ON  [YTCUAT5].[ITMMASTER]
   AFTER INSERT
AS 
BEGIN
	-- SET NOCOUNT ON added to prevent extra result sets from
	-- interfering with SELECT statements.
	SET NOCOUNT ON;
	set identity_insert YTCUAT5.TEMP_ITMMASTER on
	INSERT INTO YTCUAT5.TEMP_ITMMASTER(
	ITMREF_0,
	TSICOD_0,
	TSICOD_1,
	TSICOD_2,
	TSICOD_3,
	TSICOD_4,

	DIE_1,

	DEFAULTQTY_0,
	DOSAGE_0,
	DOSAGEG_0,
	INDICATION_0,
	DRUGCLS_0,
	DRUGTYP_0,
	ROWID)SELECT
	ITMREF_0,

	substring(TSICOD_1,1,1),
	TSICOD_2,
	TSICOD_3,
	TSICOD_4,
	DIE_0,
	DIE_1,
	DIE_2,
	DIE_3,
	DIE_4,
	ITMDES1_0,
	ITMDES2_0,
	DES4AXX_0,
	SAU_0,

	PURBASPRI_0,
	CPRAMT_0,
	CFGDELDAT_0,
	ALTBOMHDK_0,
	PLMITMREF_0,
	MINAGEMTH_0,
	DEFAULTQTY_0,
	DOSAGE_0,
	DOSAGEG_0,
	INDICATION_0,
	DRUGCLS_0,
	DRUGTYP_0,
	ROWID FROM INSERTED 
	WHERE TSICOD_1 LIKE '%WMED'
    -- Insert statements for trigger here
	set identity_insert YTCUAT5.TEMP_ITMMASTER off

	Declare @ITMREF as nvarchar(20)
	select @ITMREF = inserted.ITMREF_0 from inserted

	UPDATE ITMMASTER
	SET XPCSFLAG_0 = '1',XPCSCREATF_0 = '1'
	WHERE TSICOD_1 = 'CNMED' and ITMREF_0 = @ITMREF
END

-- =============================================
-- Author:		<Author,,Name>
-- Create date: <Create Date,,>
-- Description:	<Description,,>
-- =============================================
CREATE OR ALTER TRIGGER [YTCUAT5].[TEMP_ITMMASTER_PCS_PD]
   ON  [YTCUAT5].[ITMMASTER]
   AFTER UPDATE
AS 
BEGIN
	-- SET NOCOUNT ON added to prevent extra result sets from
	-- interfering with SELECT statements.
	SET NOCOUNT ON;
	
	DECLARE @ITMREF as nvarchar(30)
	select @ITMREF = inserted.ITMREF_0 from inserted

	IF NOT EXISTS(SELECT ITMREF_0 FROM YTCUAT5.TEMP_ITMMASTER_PCS WHERE ITMREF_0 = @ITMREF)BEGIN
	INSERT INTO YTCUAT5.TEMP_ITMMASTER_PCS(
	ITMREF_0)
	SELECT
	a.ITMREF_0
	FROM INSERTED a
	WHERE a.TSICOD_1 = 'CNMED'
	END

	IF NOT EXISTS(SELECT ITMREF_0 FROM YTCUAT5.TEMP_ITMMASTER WHERE ITMREF_0 = @ITMREF)BEGIN
	set identity_insert YTCUAT5.TEMP_ITMMASTER on
	INSERT INTO YTCUAT5.TEMP_ITMMASTER(
	ITMREF_0,
	TSICOD_0,
	TSICOD_1,
	TSICOD_2,
	TSICOD_3,
	TSICOD_4,
	DIE_0,
	DIE_1,
	DIE_2,
	DIE_3,
	DIE_4,
	ITMDES1_0,
	ITMDES2_0,
	ITMDES3_0,
	SAU_0,
	STU_0,
	SAUSTUCOE_0,
	PURBASPRI_0,
	CPRAMT_0,
	CFGDELDAT_0,
	ALTBOMHDK_0,
	PLMITMREF_0,
	MINAGEMTH_0,
	DEFAULTQTY_0,
	DOSAGE_0,
	DOSAGEG_0,
	INDICATION_0,
	DRUGCLS_0,
	DRUGTYP_0,
	ROWID)SELECT
	ITMREF_0,
	TSICOD_0,
	substring(TSICOD_1,1,1),
	TSICOD_2,
	TSICOD_3,
	TSICOD_4,
	DIE_0,
	DIE_1,
	DIE_2,
	DIE_3,
	DIE_4,
	ITMDES1_0,
	ITMDES2_0,
	DES4AXX_0,
	SAU_0,
	STU_0,
	SAUSTUCOE_0,
	PURBASPRI_0,
	CPRAMT_0,
	CFGDELDAT_0,
	ALTBOMHDK_0,
	PLMITMREF_0,
	MINAGEMTH_0,
	DEFAULTQTY_0,
	DOSAGE_0,
	DOSAGEG_0,
	INDICATION_0,
	DRUGCLS_0,
	DRUGTYP_0,
	ROWID FROM INSERTED 
	WHERE TSICOD_1 LIKE '%WMED'
	set identity_insert YTCUAT5.TEMP_ITMMASTER off
    -- Insert statements for trigger here
	END 
	IF EXISTS(SELECT ITMREF_0 FROM YTCUAT5.TEMP_ITMMASTER WHERE ITMREF_0 = @ITMREF)BEGIN
	UPDATE YTCUAT5.TEMP_ITMMASTER 
	SET 
	ITMREF_0 = b.ITMREF_0,
	TSICOD_0 = b.TSICOD_0,
	TSICOD_1 = substring(b.TSICOD_1,1,1),
	TSICOD_2 = b.TSICOD_2,
	TSICOD_3 = b.TSICOD_3,
	TSICOD_4 = b.TSICOD_4,
	DIE_0 = b.DIE_0,
	DIE_1 = b.DIE_1,
	DIE_2 = b.DIE_2,
	DIE_3 = b.DIE_3,
	DIE_4 = b.DIE_4,
	ITMDES1_0 = b.ITMDES1_0,
	ITMDES2_0 = b.ITMDES2_0,
	ITMDES3_0 = b.DES4AXX_0,
	SAU_0 =b.SAU_0,
	STU_0 =b.STU_0,
	SAUSTUCOE_0 =b.SAUSTUCOE_0,
	PURBASPRI_0 =b.PURBASPRI_0,
	CPRAMT_0 =b.CPRAMT_0,
	CFGDELDAT_0=b.CFGDELDAT_0,
	ALTBOMHDK_0=b.ALTBOMHDK_0,
	PLMITMREF_0=b.PLMITMREF_0,
	MINAGEMTH_0=b.MINAGEMTH_0,
	DEFAULTQTY_0=b.DEFAULTQTY_0,
	DOSAGE_0=b.DOSAGE_0,
	DOSAGEG_0=b.DOSAGEG_0,
	INDICATION_0=b.INDICATION_0,
	DRUGCLS_0=b.DRUGCLS_0,
	DRUGTYP_0=b.DRUGTYP_0
	FROM inserted b

	END
	

END

/****** Object:  Trigger [YTCUAT5].[STOJOU_TEMPPD]    Script Date: 29/7/2023 9:28:35 AM ******/
SET ANSI_NULLS ON

GO




-- =============================================
-- Author:		1ERP Ken Lok CPRAMT_0
-- Create date: 21/10/2022
-- Description:	Update data to temp table
-- =============================================
CREATE OR ALTER   trigger [YTCUAT5].[STOJOU_TEMPPD]
	ON [YTCUAT5].[STOJOU] 
	AFTER INSERT
AS 
BEGIN
	-- SET NOCOUNT ON added to prevent extra result sets from
	-- interfering with SELECT statements.
SET NOCOUNT ON;

	DECLARE 
		@ITMREF AS NVARCHAR(40), 
		@QTYPCU AS NUMERIC(28, 13), 
		@VCRNUM AS NVARCHAR(20)

	SELECT 
	@ITMREF = inserted.ITMREF_0,
	@QTYPCU = inserted.QTYPCU_0, 
	@VCRNUM = inserted.VCRNUM_0 
	FROM inserted

	-- 
	IF (SELECT SUM(QTYPCU_0) FROM YTCUAT5.STOJOU WHERE VCRNUM_0 = @VCRNUM AND ITMREF_0 = @ITMREF ) = 0
	BEGIN
		SET IDENTITY_INSERT YTCUAT5.TEMP_STOJOU ON
		INSERT INTO YTCUAT5.TEMP_STOJOU 
		( BPRNUM_0, VCRNUM_0, QTYPCU_0, UPDDATTIM_0, SHLDAT_0, CPRAMT_0, CHECK_NUM, ITMREF_0, ITMDES1_0, ITMDES2_0, ROWID )
		SELECT 
		a.BPRNUM_0, a.VCRNUM_0, 0, a.UPDDATTIM_0, c.SHLDAT_0, a.VARORD_0, 2, a.ITMREF_0, b.ITMDES1_0, b.ITMDES2_0, a.ROWID
		FROM INSERTED a
		JOIN YTCUAT5.ITMMASTER b ON a.ITMREF_0 = b.ITMREF_0
		JOIN YTCUAT5.STOLOT c ON a.ITMREF_0 = c.ITMREF_0 AND a.LOT_0 = c.LOT_0 AND a.SLO_0 = c.SLO_0
		WHERE b.TSICOD_1 LIKE '%WMED' AND a.QTYPCU_0 > 0 AND a.STA_0 = 'A' AND a.TRSTYP_0 = '2'
		SET IDENTITY_INSERT YTCUAT5.TEMP_STOJOU OFF
	END

	IF (SELECT COUNT(*) FROM YTCUAT5.STOJOU WHERE VCRNUM_0 = @VCRNUM and ITMREF_0 = @ITMREF) = 1 
	BEGIN
		SET IDENTITY_INSERT YTCUAT5.TEMP_STOJOU ON
		INSERT INTO YTCUAT5.TEMP_STOJOU
		( BPRNUM_0, VCRNUM_0, QTYPCU_0, UPDDATTIM_0, SHLDAT_0, CPRAMT_0, CHECK_NUM, ITMREF_0, ITMDES1_0, ITMDES2_0, ROWID )
		SELECT 
		a.BPRNUM_0, a.VCRNUM_0, a.QTYPCU_0, a.UPDDATTIM_0, c.SHLDAT_0, a.VARORD_0, 0, a.ITMREF_0, b.ITMDES1_0, b.ITMDES2_0, a.ROWID
		FROM INSERTED a
		JOIN YTCUAT5.ITMMASTER b ON a.ITMREF_0 = b.ITMREF_0
		JOIN YTCUAT5.STOLOT c ON a.ITMREF_0 = c.ITMREF_0 and a.LOT_0 = c.LOT_0 and a.SLO_0 = c.SLO_0
		WHERE b.TSICOD_1 LIKE '%WMED' and a.QTYPCU_0 < 0 and a.STA_0 = 'A' and a.TRSTYP_0 = '2'
		SET IDENTITY_INSERT YTCUAT5.TEMP_STOJOU OFF
	END
	ELSE 
	BEGIN
		SET IDENTITY_INSERT YTCUAT5.TEMP_STOJOU ON
		INSERT INTO YTCUAT5.TEMP_STOJOU(
		BPRNUM_0,
		VCRNUM_0,
		QTYPCU_0,
		UPDDATTIM_0,
		SHLDAT_0,
		CPRAMT_0,
		CHECK_NUM,
		ITMREF_0,
		ITMDES1_0,
		ITMDES2_0,
		ROWID	
		)
		SELECT 
		a.BPRNUM_0, a.VCRNUM_0, a.QTYPCU_0, a.UPDDATTIM_0, c.SHLDAT_0, a.VARORD_0, 2, a.ITMREF_0, b.ITMDES1_0, b.ITMDES2_0, a.ROWID
		FROM INSERTED a
		JOIN YTCUAT5.ITMMASTER b ON a.ITMREF_0 = b.ITMREF_0
		JOIN YTCUAT5.STOLOT c ON a.ITMREF_0 = c.ITMREF_0 AND a.LOT_0 = c.LOT_0 AND a.SLO_0 = c.SLO_0
		WHERE 
			b.TSICOD_1 LIKE '%WMED' AND 
			(a.QTYPCU_0 < 0 OR a.QTYPCU_0 = 0) AND 
			a.STA_0 = 'A' and 
			a.TRSTYP_0 = '2'
		SET IDENTITY_INSERT YTCUAT5.TEMP_STOJOU OFF
	END

	--set identity_insert YTCUAT5.TEMP_STOJOU on
	--INSERT INTO YTCUAT5.TEMP_STOJOU(
	--BPRNUM_0,
	--VCRNUM_0,
	--QTYPCU_0,
	--UPDDATTIM_0,
	--SHLDAT_0,
	--CPRAMT_0,
	--CHECK_NUM,
	--ITMREF_0,
	--ITMDES1_0,
	--ITMDES2_0,
	--ROWID	
	--)SELECT 
	--a.BPRNUM_0,
	--a.VCRNUM_0,
	--a.QTYPCU_0,
	--a.UPDDATTIM_0,
	--c.SHLDAT_0,
	--a.VARORD_0,
	--1,
	--a.ITMREF_0,
	--b.ITMDES1_0,
	--b.ITMDES2_0,
	--a.ROWID
	--FROM INSERTED a
	--join YTCUAT5.ITMMASTER b on a.ITMREF_0 = b.ITMREF_0
	--join YTCUAT5.STOLOT c on a.ITMREF_0 = c.ITMREF_0 and a.LOT_0 = c.LOT_0 and a.SLO_0 = c.SLO_0
	--where b.TSICOD_1 like '%WMED' and a.QTYPCU_0 > 0 and a.STA_0 = 'A' and a.TRSTYP_0 = '2'and a.REGFLG_0 = '2'
	--set identity_insert YTCUAT5.TEMP_STOJOU off
	IF (SELECT COUNT(*) FROM YTCUAT5.STOJOU WHERE VCRNUM_0 = @VCRNUM and ITMREF_0 = @ITMREF) = 1 
	BEGIN
		UPDATE YTCUAT5.STOJOU
		SET XPCSFLAG_0 = '1',XPCSREVERSE_0 = '0'
		FROM YTCUAT5.STOJOU a
		JOIN YTCUAT5.ITMMASTER b on a.ITMREF_0 = b.ITMREF_0
		WHERE b.TSICOD_1 = 'CNMED' and a.ITMREF_0 = @ITMREF and @QTYPCU < 0 and a.STA_0 = 'A' and a.TRSTYP_0 = '2' and a.REGFLG_0 = '1' and a.VCRNUM_0 = @VCRNUM
	END
	ELSE
	BEGIN
		UPDATE YTCUAT5.STOJOU
		SET XPCSFLAG_0 = '1',XPCSREVERSE_0 = '1'
		FROM YTCUAT5.STOJOU a
		JOIN YTCUAT5.ITMMASTER b on a.ITMREF_0 = b.ITMREF_0
		WHERE b.TSICOD_1 = 'CNMED' and a.ITMREF_0 = @ITMREF and @QTYPCU < 0 and a.STA_0 = 'A' and a.TRSTYP_0 = '2' and a.REGFLG_0 = '2' and a.VCRNUM_0 = @VCRNUM

		UPDATE YTCUAT5.STOJOU
		SET XPCSFLAG_0 = '1',XPCSREVERSE_0 = '1'
		FROM YTCUAT5.STOJOU a
		JOIN YTCUAT5.ITMMASTER b on a.ITMREF_0 = b.ITMREF_0
		WHERE b.TSICOD_1 = 'CNMED' and a.ITMREF_0 = @ITMREF and @QTYPCU > 0 and a.STA_0 = 'A' and a.TRSTYP_0 = '2' and a.VCRNUM_0 = @VCRNUM
	END

END
GO

ALTER TABLE [YTCUAT5].[STOJOU] ENABLE TRIGGER [STOJOU_TEMPPD]
GO

/****** Object:  Trigger [YTCUAT5].[STOJOU_TEMP_DELETEPD]    Script Date: 29/7/2023 9:28:51 AM ******/

-- =============================================
-- Author:		1ERP Ken Lok CPRAMT_0
-- Create date: 21/10/2022
-- Description:	Update data to temp table
-- =============================================
CREATE OR ALTER trigger [YTCUAT5].[STOJOU_TEMP_DELETEPD]
	ON [YTCUAT5].[STOJOU] 
	AFTER DELETE
AS 
BEGIN
	-- SET NOCOUNT ON added to prevent extra result sets from
	-- interfering with SELECT statements.
SET NOCOUNT ON;
set identity_insert YTCUAT5.TEMP_STOJOU on
	INSERT INTO YTCUAT5.TEMP_STOJOU(
	BPRNUM_0,
	VCRNUM_0,
	QTYPCU_0,
	UPDDATTIM_0,
	SHLDAT_0,
	CPRAMT_0,
	CHECK_NUM,
	ITMREF_0,
	ITMDES1_0,
	ITMDES2_0,
	ROWID	
	)SELECT 
	a.BPRNUM_0,
	a.VCRNUM_0,
	a.QTYPCU_0,
	a.UPDDATTIM_0,
	c.SHLDAT_0,
	b.CPRAMT_0,
	1,
	a.ITMREF_0,
	b.ITMDES1_0,
	b.ITMDES2_0,
	a.ROWID
	FROM INSERTED a
	join YTCUAT5.ITMMASTER b on a.ITMREF_0 = b.ITMREF_0
	join YTCUAT5.STOLOT c on a.ITMREF_0 = c.ITMREF_0 and a.LOT_0 = c.LOT_0 and a.SLO_0 = c.SLO_0 
	where b.TSICOD_1 like '%WMED' and a.STA_0 = 'A' and a.TRSTYP_0 = '2'
set identity_insert YTCUAT5.TEMP_STOJOU off

	
	Declare @ITMREF as nvarchar(40)
	select @ITMREF = inserted.ITMREF_0 from inserted

	Declare @QTYPCU as numeric(28, 13)
	select @QTYPCU = inserted.QTYPCU_0 from inserted


	UPDATE YTCUAT5.STOJOU
	SET XPCSFLAG_0 = '1',XPCSREVERSE_0 = '1'
	FROM YTCUAT5.STOJOU a
	JOIN YTCUAT5.ITMMASTER b on a.ITMREF_0 = b.ITMREF_0
	WHERE b.TSICOD_1 = 'CNMED' and a.ITMREF_0 = @ITMREF and @QTYPCU > 0 and a.STA_0 = 'A' and TRSTYP_0 = '2'
END
GO

ALTER TABLE [YTCUAT5].[STOJOU] ENABLE TRIGGER [STOJOU_TEMP_DELETEPD]
GO


USE [x3erpv12]
GO

SET ANSI_NULLS ON

SET QUOTED_IDENTIFIER ON

CREATE OR ALTER Trigger  
 [YTCUAT5].[STOJOU_DEL] 
 On [YTCUAT5].[STOJOU] 
 After DELETE

  set @datsys = getdate() 
  set @hh = datename(hour,@datsys) 
  set @mm = datename(minute,@datsys) 
  set @ss = datename(second,@datsys) 
  If len(@hh)=1 set @hh = '0'+@hh 
  If len(@mm)=1 set @mm = '0'+@mm 
  If len(@ss)=1 set @ss = '0'+@ss 
  set @heusys = @hh+@mm+@ss 
  set @datsys = cast((cast(@datsys as date)) as datetime)
